+                    if interval_us_sel in ["1?쒓컙 (60 Minute)", "30遺?(30 Minute)", "10遺?(10 Minute)", "5遺?(5 Minute)", "3遺?(3 Minute)", "1遺?(1 Minute)"]:
+                        df_final = df_us.sort_index()
+                    else:
+                        int_map = {"?쇰큺 (Daily)": "D", "二쇰큺 (Weekly)": "W", "?붾큺 (Monthly)": "M", "?곕큺 (Yearly)": "Y"}
+                        period_code = int_map[interval_us_sel]
+                        
+                        if period_code == "D":

+                    
+                    st.dataframe(df_final)

+                    run_analysis_and_prompts(df_final, us_ticker, name_diplay, "US", "USD", interval_us_sel, key_suffix="us_single")
+            else:

+import streamlit as st
+from datetime import datetime, timedelta
+
+@st.fragment
+def date_selector_fragment(prefix, default_start, default_end, interval_sel):
+    """
+    Renders the date selection UI.
+    Updates st.session_state directly.
+    Runs in a fragment to prevent full app rerun on interaction.
+    """
+    manual_dates = st.checkbox("湲곌컙 吏곸젒 ?ㅼ젙 (Manual Date Range)", value=False, key=f"{prefix}_manual_dates_checkbox")
+    
+    # Logic to determine effective dates
+    final_start = default_start
+    final_end = default_end
+    
+    if manual_dates:
+         col_d1, col_d2 = st.columns(2)
+         with col_d1:
+             final_start = st.date_input("?쒖옉??(Start)", default_start, key=f"{prefix}_start_input")
+         with col_d2:
+             final_end = st.date_input("醫낅즺??(End)", default_end, key=f"{prefix}_end_input")
+    else:
+         final_end = default_end
+         
+         # Auto Logic
+         duration_text = "1??(1 Year)"
+         
+         if "?꾩껜" in interval_sel or "All" in interval_sel or "醫낇빀遺꾩꽍" in interval_sel:
+             final_start = datetime(1990, 1, 1)
+             duration_text = "?꾩껜 援ш컙 (Multi-Timeframe Analysis)"
+         elif "1遺? in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end
+             duration_text = "1??(1 Day)"
+         elif "3遺? in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=2)
+             duration_text = "2??(2 Days)"
+         elif "5遺? in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=4)
+             duration_text = "4??(4 Days)"
+         elif "10遺? in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=7)
+             duration_text = "7??(1 Week)"
+         elif "30遺? in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=14)
+             duration_text = "14??(2 Weeks)"
+         elif "1?쒓컙" in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=29)
+             duration_text = "??1媛쒖썡 (1 Month)"
+         elif "二쇰큺" in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=3650) 
+             duration_text = "10??(10 Years)"
+         elif "?붾큺" in interval_sel or "?곕큺" in interval_sel: 
+             final_start = datetime(1990, 1, 1) 
+             duration_text = "?곸옣 ?댄썑 ?꾩껜 (Max)"
+         else: 
+             final_start = final_end - timedelta(days=365) # Daily default
+             duration_text = "1??(1 Year)"
+             
+         st.info(f"?뮕 遺꾩꽍 媛꾧꺽???곕Ⅸ 理쒖쟻 湲곌컙({duration_text})???먮룞?쇰줈 ?곸슜?⑸땲?? (蹂寃쏀븯?ㅻ㈃ ??泥댄겕諛뺤뒪 ?좏깮)")
+    
+    # Update Session State for Main App to use
+    st.session_state[f"{prefix}_start"] = final_start
+    st.session_state[f"{prefix}_end"] = final_end

+def generate_multi_timeframe_gemini_prompt(ticker, name, market, currency, timeframe_dfs, news_list=None):
+    """
+    Generates a COMPREHENSIVE prompt for Gemini to analyze multiple timeframes.
+    
+    Args:
+        timeframe_dfs (dict): {'Daily': df_d, 'Weekly': df_w, 'Monthly': df_m, 'Yearly': df_y}
+    """
+    
+    # Format Tables
+    tables_str = ""
+    for tf, df in timeframe_dfs.items():
+        if not df.empty:
+            # Taking recent rows to keep prompt size manageable
+            # Daily: last 30, Weekly: last 20, Monthly: last 24, Yearly: All
+            if tf == 'Daily': df_slice = df.tail(30)
+            elif tf == 'Weekly': df_slice = df.tail(20)
+            elif tf == 'Monthly': df_slice = df.tail(24)
+            else: df_slice = df
+            
+            csv_data = df_slice.to_csv(index=True)
+            tables_str += f"\n[{tf.upper()}_DATA (Recent)]\n{csv_data}\n"
+
+    # Format News
+    news_str = ""
+    if news_list and len(news_list) > 0:
+        for n in news_list:
+            news_str += f"{n.get('date', '')} | {n.get('title', '')} | {n.get('source', '')} | {n.get('link', '')}\n"
+    else:
+        news_str = "(?댁뒪 ?곗씠?곌? ?놁뒿?덈떎.)"
+
+    prompt = f"""
+2) Gemini???꾨＼?꾪듃 (Multi-Timeframe ?듯빀 遺꾩꽍)
+
+[ROLE]
+?뱀떊? 二쇱떇 ?쒖옣??"硫????꾪봽?덉엫(Multi-Timeframe) 湲곗닠??遺꾩꽍 ?꾨Ц媛"?낅땲??
+?쒓났???쇰큺(Daily), 二쇰큺(Weekly), ?붾큺(Monthly), ?곕큺(Yearly) ?곗씠?곕? 醫낇빀?섏뿬, ?④린/以묎린/?κ린 異붿꽭???뺥빀?깆쓣 ?됯??섍퀬 理쒖쟻??留ㅻℓ ?꾨왂???섎┰?⑸땲??
+
+[GOAL]
+4媛吏 ??꾪봽?덉엫???곗씠?곕? 遺꾩꽍?섏뿬 ?섎굹???듯빀 由ы룷?몃? ?묒꽦?섏꽭??
+?뱁엳 "??異붿꽭(?곕큺/?붾큺)媛 ?댁븘?덈뒗媛?", "以묎린 議곗젙(二쇰큺)??留덈Т由щ릺?덈뒗媛?", "?④린 吏꾩엯 ?쒖젏(?쇰큺)?멸??"瑜??먮떒?섎뒗 寃껋씠 ?듭떖?낅땲??
+
+[INPUT DATA]
+- Ticker: {ticker} ({name})
+- Market: {market}

+
+{tables_str}
+
+[NEWS]
+{news_str}
+
+[OUTPUT FORMAT]
+1. **醫낇빀 ?곗씠???붿빟**:
+   - ?곕큺/?붾큺: ?κ린 異붿꽭 (?곸듅/?섎씫/?〓낫) 諛??듭떖 吏吏/???+   - 二쇰큺: 以묎린 異붿꽭 諛??⑦꽩
+   - ?쇰큺: ?④린 異붿꽭 諛?嫄곕옒???뱀씠?ы빆

+   {{
+      "meta": {{"ticker": "{ticker}", "name": "{name}"}},
+      "overall_outlook": "bullish|bearish|neutral",

+          "weekly": "bullish|bearish|neutral",
+          "daily": "bullish|bearish|neutral"
+      }},
+      "score": 0,  // -10 to +10
+      "strategy": {{

+"""
+    return prompt

+def generate_gemini_prompt(ticker, name, market, currency, timeframe, df, news_list=None, holding_status="愿留?以묐┰)", avg_price=None, start_dt_str=None, end_dt_str=None):

+    """

+    csv_data = df.to_csv(index=True)

+    else:

+
+    # Holding Status Logic

+         if avg_price is not None and avg_price > 0:

+             if currency == "USD":

+             else:

+             holding_advice = f"?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀 以?*?대ŉ, **?됰떒媛??{price_str}**?낅땲?? ???됰떒媛瑜?湲곗??쇰줈 理쒖슦?좎쟻?쇰줈 **泥?궛(?듭젅/?먯젅) ?먮뒗 臾쇳?湲???대컢**???〓뒗 寃껋뿉 吏묒쨷?섏꽭??"
+         else:
+             holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀 以?*?낅땲?? 理쒖슦?좎쟻?쇰줈 **泥?궛(?듭젅/?먯젅) ??대컢**???〓뒗 寃껋뿉 吏묒쨷?섏꽭??"
+    elif "誘몃낫?? in holding_status:
+         holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀?섍퀬 ?덉? ?딆뒿?덈떎**. **?좉퇋 留ㅼ닔 吏꾩엯**???좏슚?쒖?, ?좏슚?섎떎硫??곸젅??媛寃⑸????대뵒?몄? 遺꾩꽍?섏꽭??"
+    else:

+
+    prompt = f"""

+- **?ъ옄???곹깭 諛섏쁺**: {holding_advice}

+媛?ν븯硫?寃??湲곕뒫???ъ슜?댁꽌 ?쒖턀洹?14?쇄??댁뒪 10~20媛쒕? ?섏쭛?섍퀬,

+2) 諛⑸쾿濡좊퀎 ?좏샇(異붿꽭/紐⑤찘?/蹂?숈꽦/吏吏???嫄곕옒??李⑦듃 ?⑦꽩 遺꾩꽍(?ㅻ뱶?ㅼ늻?? ?띾컮????) 媛곴컖 ?먯닔(-2~+2)
+3) ?댁뒪 ?대깽??由ъ뒪???쒓퉭??+ ?듭떖 5以??붿빟)
+4) 醫낇빀 ?ㅼ퐫??媛以묒튂 怨듦컻)? 理쒖쥌 ?≪뀡(buy/wait/sell)

+def generate_multi_timeframe_gemini_prompt(ticker, name, market, currency, timeframe_dfs, news_list=None, holding_status="愿留?以묐┰)", avg_price=None, start_dt_str=None, end_dt_str=None):
+    """
+    Generates a COMPREHENSIVE prompt for Gemini to analyze multiple timeframes.
+    
+    Args:
+        timeframe_dfs (dict): {'Daily': df_d, 'Weekly': df_w, 'Monthly': df_m, 'Yearly': df_y}
+        holding_status (str): User's current position status.
+    """
+    
+    # Format Tables
+    tables_str = ""
+    for tf, df in timeframe_dfs.items():
+        if not df.empty:
+            # Taking recent rows to keep prompt size manageable, but enough for indicators
+            # Daily: last 60, Weekly: last 52, Monthly: last 36, Yearly: All
+            if tf == 'Daily': df_slice = df.tail(60)
+            elif tf == 'Weekly': df_slice = df.tail(52)
+            elif tf == 'Monthly': df_slice = df.tail(36)
+            else: df_slice = df
+            
+            csv_data = df_slice.to_csv(index=True)
+            tables_str += f"\n[{tf.upper()}_DATA (Recent)]\n{csv_data}\n"
+
+    # Format News
+    news_str = ""
+    if news_list and len(news_list) > 0:
+        for n in news_list:
+            news_str += f"{n.get('date', '')} | {n.get('title', '')} | {n.get('source', '')} | {n.get('link', '')}\n"
+    else:
+        news_str = "(?댁뒪 ?곗씠?곌? ?놁뒿?덈떎.)"
+
+    # Holding Status Logic
+    holding_advice = ""
+    if "蹂댁쑀" in holding_status and "留ㅻ룄" in holding_status:
+         if avg_price is not None and avg_price > 0:
+             curr_unit = "?? if currency == "KRW" else "$"
+             if currency == "USD": 
+                 price_str = f"{curr_unit}{avg_price:,.2f}"
+             else:
+                 price_str = f"{avg_price:,.0f}{curr_unit}"
+             holding_advice = f"?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀 以?*?대ŉ, **?됰떒媛??{price_str}**?낅땲?? ???됰떒媛瑜?湲곗??쇰줈 理쒖슦?좎쟻?쇰줈 **泥?궛(?듭젅/?먯젅) ?먮뒗 臾쇳?湲???대컢**???〓뒗 寃껋뿉 吏묒쨷?섏꽭??"
+         else:
+             holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀 以?*?낅땲?? 理쒖슦?좎쟻?쇰줈 **泥?궛(?듭젅/?먯젅) ??대컢**???〓뒗 寃껋뿉 吏묒쨷?섏꽭??"
+    elif "誘몃낫?? in holding_status:
+         holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??**蹂댁쑀?섍퀬 ?덉? ?딆뒿?덈떎**. **?좉퇋 留ㅼ닔 吏꾩엯**???좏슚?쒖?, ?좏슚?섎떎硫??곸젅??媛寃⑸????대뵒?몄? 遺꾩꽍?섏꽭??"
+    else:
+         holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 **愿留?以묐┰)** ?곹깭?낅땲?? 諛⑺뼢?깆씠 ?뺤떎?댁쭏 ?뚭퉴吏 湲곕떎?ㅼ빞 ?좎?, ?꾨땲硫?吏湲??됰룞?댁빞 ?좎? 媛앷??곸쑝濡?遺꾩꽍?섏꽭??"
+
+    prompt = f"""
+2) Gemini???꾨＼?꾪듃 (Multi-Timeframe ?듯빀 遺꾩꽍)
+
+[ROLE]
+?뱀떊? 二쇱떇 ?쒖옣??"硫????꾪봽?덉엫(Multi-Timeframe) 湲곗닠??遺꾩꽍 ?꾨Ц媛"?낅땲??
+?쒓났???쇰큺(Daily), 二쇰큺(Weekly), ?붾큺(Monthly), ?곕큺(Yearly) ?곗씠?곕? 醫낇빀?섏뿬, ?④린/以묎린/?κ린 異붿꽭???뺥빀?깆쓣 ?됯??섍퀬 理쒖쟻??留ㅻℓ ?꾨왂???섎┰?⑸땲??
+

+def generate_multi_timeframe_chatgpt_prompt(ticker, name, market, currency, timeframe_dfs, news_list=None, holding_status="愿留?以묐┰)", avg_price=None, start_dt_str=None, end_dt_str=None):
+    """
+    Generates a COMPREHENSIVE prompt for ChatGPT to analyze multiple timeframes.
+    
+    Args:
+        timeframe_dfs (dict): {'Daily': df_d, 'Weekly': df_w, 'Monthly': df_m, 'Yearly': df_y}
+        holding_status (str): User's current position status.
+    """
+    
+    # Format Tables
+    tables_str = ""
+    for tf, df in timeframe_dfs.items():
+        if not df.empty:
+            if tf == 'Daily': df_slice = df.tail(60)
+            elif tf == 'Weekly': df_slice = df.tail(52)
+            elif tf == 'Monthly': df_slice = df.tail(36)
+            else: df_slice = df
+            
+            csv_data = df_slice.to_csv(index=True)
+            tables_str += f"\n[{tf.upper()}_DATA (Recent)]\n{csv_data}\n"
+
+    # Format News
+    news_str = ""
+    if news_list and len(news_list) > 0:
+        for n in news_list:
+            news_str += f"{n.get('date', '')} | {n.get('title', '')} | {n.get('source', '')} | {n.get('link', '')}\n"
+    else:
+        news_str = "(?댁뒪 ?곗씠?곌? ?놁뒿?덈떎.)"
+
+    # Holding Status Logic
+    holding_advice = ""
+    if "蹂댁쑀" in holding_status and "留ㅻ룄" in holding_status:
+         if avg_price is not None and avg_price > 0:
+             curr_unit = "?? if currency == "KRW" else "$"
+             if currency == "USD": 
+                 price_str = f"{curr_unit}{avg_price:,.2f}"
+             else:
+                 price_str = f"{avg_price:,.0f}{curr_unit}"
+             holding_advice = f"?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??'蹂댁쑀 以??대ŉ, ?됰떒媛??**{price_str}**?낅땲?? ???됰떒媛瑜?湲곗??쇰줈 ?섏씡 ?ㅽ쁽(?듭젅), 臾쇳?湲? ?먯넀????대컢?????紐낇솗???꾨왂???쒖떆?섏꽭??"
+         else:
+             holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??'蹂댁쑀 以??낅땲?? 泥?궛(?듭젅/?먯젅) ??대컢?????紐낇솗???꾨왂???쒖떆?섏꽭??"
+    elif "誘몃낫?? in holding_status:
+         holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 ??醫낅ぉ??'誘몃낫?? ?곹깭?낅땲?? ?좉퇋 吏꾩엯 留ㅼ닔?먭낵 ?꾨왂??吏묒쨷?섏꽭??"
+    else:
+         holding_advice = "?ъ슜?먮뒗 ?꾩옱 '愿留? 以묒엯?덈떎. 媛앷???諛⑺뼢?깃낵 ?뺤씤 留ㅻℓ 湲곗????덈궡?섏꽭??"
+
+    prompt = f"""
+1) ChatGPT???꾨＼?꾪듃 (Multi-Timeframe ?듯빀 遺꾩꽍)
+
+[ROLE]
+?뱀떊? "硫????꾪봽?덉엫(Multi-Timeframe) 湲곗닠??遺꾩꽍 ?꾨Ц媛"?낅땲??
+?쒓났???쇰큺/二쇰큺/?붾큺/?곕큺 ?곗씠?곕? 醫낇빀?섏뿬, ??以??κ린 異붿꽭???뺥빀?깆쓣 ?됯??섍퀬 理쒖쟻 留ㅻℓ ?꾨왂???섎┰?섏꽭??
+
+[INPUT DATA]
+- Ticker: {ticker} ({name})
+- Market: {market}
+- Timeframes Provided: {', '.join(timeframe_dfs.keys())}
+- **Data Range (Daily)**: {start_dt_str} ~ {end_dt_str}
+- **Investor Status**: {holding_status}
+- **Investor Advice**: {holding_advice}
+
+{tables_str}
+
+[NEWS]
+{news_str}
+
+[OUTPUT FORMAT]
+?꾨옒 ?뱀뀡??紐낇솗??援щ텇?섏뿬 ?쒓?濡??곸꽭 由ы룷???묒꽦:
+
+1. **醫낇빀 ?곗씠???붿빟 (遺꾩꽍 ?곗씠??湲곌컙: {start_dt_str} ~ {end_dt_str} 諛섎뱶??紐낆떆)**: ??異붿꽭(???곕큺)遺???몃? 異붿꽭(二??쇰큺)濡??섑뼢??Top-down) ?붿빟
+2. **硫????꾪봽?덉엫 ?뺥빀??遺꾩꽍**: ?κ린??異붿꽭? ?④린 ?먮쫫???숈“??異⑸룎 ?щ? 泥댄겕
+3. **?듭떖 媛寃??덈꺼, 吏??(異붿꽭, 紐⑤찘? ?? 諛?李⑦듃 ?⑦꽩 遺꾩꽍 (?ㅻ뱶?ㅼ늻?? ?띾컮????**
+4. **理쒖쥌 留ㅻℓ ?꾨왂 (Status: {holding_status})**:
+   - **議곗뼵**: {holding_advice}
+   - **?ㅽ뻾 怨꾪쉷**: 援ъ껜??吏꾩엯, ?먯젅, 紐⑺몴 踰붿쐞 ?쒖떆
+5. **JSON ?щ㎎ ?붿빟 (遺꾩꽍 寃곌낵 ?뚯떛??**:
+   ```json
+   {{
+      "meta": {{"ticker": "{ticker}", "name": "{name}"}},
+      "timeframe_analysis": {{"yearly": "","monthly": "","weekly": "","daily": ""}},
+      "action": "buy|sell|wait",
+      "entry_zone": [], "stop_loss": 0, "targets": []
+   }}
+   ```
+"""
+    return prompt

+import pandas as pd
+import requests
+import io
+
+def get_sp500_mapping():
+    """Fetches S&P 500 tickers and names from Wikipedia."""
+    try:
+        url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S%26P_500_companies'
+        headers = {
+            'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'
+        }
+        print(f"Requesting {url}...")
+        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers)
+        r.raise_for_status()
+        
+        print("Parsing HTML...")
+        dfs = pd.read_html(io.StringIO(r.text))
+        df = dfs[0]
+        
+        print(f"Columns: {df.columns}")
+        
+        # Check expected columns
+        if 'Symbol' not in df.columns or 'Security' not in df.columns:
+             print("Mapping columns not found.")
+             return {}
+             
+        mapping = dict(zip(df['Symbol'], df['Security']))
+        return mapping
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+        return {}
+
+m = get_sp500_mapping()
+print(f"Mapped {len(m)} companies.")
+if m:
+    first_5 = list(m.items())[:5]
+    print("Sample:", first_5)

+import pandas as pd
+import numpy as np
+
+def calculate_indicators(df):
+    """
+    Calculates technical indicators using standard pandas functions.
+    Expects df to have 'Close' column.
+    Returns df with added columns: SMA_20, SMA_60, RSI_14, MACD, BB_Upper, BB_Lower.
+    """
+    if df is None or df.empty:
+        return df
+    
+    # Ensure Index is Datetime
+    if not isinstance(df.index, pd.DatetimeIndex):
+        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)
+
+    # Make a copy to avoid SettingWithCopy warnings on the original dataframe slice if applicable
+    df = df.copy()
+
+    # 1. Moving Averages
+    df['SMA_20'] = df['Close'].rolling(window=20).mean()
+    df['SMA_60'] = df['Close'].rolling(window=60).mean()
+    
+    # 2. RSI (Relative Strength Index)
+    delta = df['Close'].diff()
+    gain = (delta.where(delta > 0, 0))
+    loss = (-delta.where(delta < 0, 0))
+    
+    avg_gain = gain.rolling(window=14).mean()
+    avg_loss = loss.rolling(window=14).mean()
+    
+    rs = avg_gain / avg_loss
+    df['RSI_14'] = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
+    
+    # Fill NaN caused by division by zero if any (though rare in stock prices)
+    df['RSI_14'] = df['RSI_14'].fillna(50) 
+
+    # 3. MACD
+    # EMA 12
+    k12 = df['Close'].ewm(span=12, adjust=False).mean()
+    # EMA 26
+    k26 = df['Close'].ewm(span=26, adjust=False).mean()
+    
+    df['MACD'] = k12 - k26
+    # Signal line (often not displayed but needed for full macd, here we just return MACD line as per request or usage)
+    # df['MACD_Signal'] = df['MACD'].ewm(span=9, adjust=False).mean()
+        
+    # 4. Bollinger Bands
+    # Middle Band = 20 SMA
+    # Upper Band = 20 SMA + (20 SD * 2)
+    # Lower Band = 20 SMA - (20 SD * 2)
+    std_20 = df['Close'].rolling(window=20).std()
+    
+    df['BB_Upper'] = df['SMA_20'] + (std_20 * 2)
+    df['BB_Lower'] = df['SMA_20'] - (std_20 * 2)
+        
+    return df
+
+def resample_ohlcv(df, period):
+    """
+    Resamples OHLCV data to a different period.
+    period: 'W' (Weekly), 'M' (Monthly), 'D' (Daily - returns copy)
+    """
+    if period == 'D':
+        return df.copy()
+        
+    # Validation: Ensure index is Datetime
+    if not isinstance(df.index, pd.DatetimeIndex):
+        df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)
+
+    # Resampling Logic
+    # Open: first, High: max, Low: min, Close: last, Volume: sum
+    # Note: Column names must match app.py (Open, High, Low, Close, Volume)
+    agg_dict = {
+        'Open': 'first',
+        'High': 'max',
+        'Low': 'min',
+        'Close': 'last',
+        'Volume': 'sum'
+    }
+    
+    # Handle case where some cols might be missing
+    existing_agg = {k: v for k, v in agg_dict.items() if k in df.columns}
+    
+    resampled = df.resample(period).agg(existing_agg)
+    resampled = resampled.dropna() # Remove empty periods
+    
+    return resampled
